    <!-- loading Javascript for using the persistence Service -->
    <script src="//unpkg.com/@theidentityselector/thiss-ds"></script>

    <script type="text/javascript">

        var SeamlessAccessService = {
            spUrl: "/action/ssostart",
            returnURL: window.location.href,
            my_context: 'seamlessaccess.org',
            timeout: 5000,

            getWAYFLessUrl: function (entityId) {
                return this.spUrl + "?idp=" + encodeURIComponent(entityId)
                    + "&redirectUri=" + encodeURIComponent(this.returnURL);
            },
            retrieveEntity: function (ms) {
                var self = this;
                var persistService = new thiss.PersistenceService('https://service.seamlessaccess.org/ps/');

                if(ms == undefined || ms === ''){
                    ms = this.timeout;
                }

                return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
                    persistService.entities(self.my_context)
                        .then(function (res) {
                            // get the results
                            var results = res.data;
                            return resolve(results);
                        }, function (err) {
                            // failed
                            reject('retrieve entity error: ' + err);
                        });
                    // Set up the timeout
                    setTimeout(function() {
                        reject('Promise timed out ' + ms + ' ms');
                    }, ms);
                });
            },
            updateEntity: function (entitydata) {
                var self = this;
                var persistService =  new thiss.PersistenceService('https://service.seamlessaccess.org/ps/');

                var jsonObj = {};
                try {
                    //try to parse it, if it is a json string
                    jsonObj = JSON.parse(entitydata.val());
                } catch (e) {
                    jsonObj = entitydata;
                }
                return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
                    persistService.update(self.my_context, jsonObj)
                        .then(function (res) {
                            // Process the results
                            var ssoInstitutions = res.data;
                            return resolve(ssoInstitutions);
                        }, function (err) {
                            // failed
                            console.log('failed to update the local storage duo to: ' + err);
                            reject(err);
                        });
                })
            },
            removeEntity: function (entityId) {
                var self = this;
                var persistService =  new thiss.PersistenceService('https://service.seamlessaccess.org/ps/');

                return new Promise(function (resolve) {
                    persistService.remove(self.my_context, entityId)
                        .then(function (res) {
                            return resolve(res);
                        }, function (err) {
                            // failed
                            console.log('failed to remove from local storage duo to: ' + err);
                        });
                })
            },
            getAccessibleEntityStatus: function (doi, entityId) {
                return new Promise(function (resolve) {
                    $.ajax({
                        type: 'POST',
                        url: '/action/seamlessAccess',
                        accept: {
                            text: "application/json"
                        },
                        data: {doi: doi, entityid: entityId}

                    }).done(function (status) {
                        return resolve(status);
                    });
                });
            },
            getEntitiesWithAllInfo: function (doi) {
                let self = this,
                    arrayOfPromises = [];
                return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
                    self.retrieveEntity().then(function (res) {
                        let allSsoInstitutions = res;
                        for (i = 0; i < allSsoInstitutions.length; i++) {
                            let ssoInstitution = allSsoInstitutions[i];
                            arrayOfPromises.push(new Promise(function (resolve) {
                                self.getAccessibleEntityStatus(doi, ssoInstitution.entity.entityID)
                                    .then(function (entityStatus) {
                                        resolve({
                                            entityID: ssoInstitution.entity.entityID,
                                            entityTitle: ssoInstitution.entity.title,
                                            entityStatusObj: entityStatus,
                                            entitySsoUrl: self.getWAYFLessUrl(ssoInstitution.entity.entityID)
                                        });
                                    }, function (err) {
                                        console.log('failed to get the entity status: ' + err);
                                    });
                            }));
                        }
                        Promise.all(arrayOfPromises)
                            .then(function (finalResponse) {
                                resolve(finalResponse);
                            });

                    }).catch(function (err) {
                        reject(err);
                    })
                });
            }
        };

        window.addEventListener('load', function () {
            document.querySelectorAll(".sso-institution").forEach(function (institution) {
                var entityId = institution.getAttribute('data-entityid');
                var entityName = institution.getAttribute('data-name');
                var entitydata = {
                    entityID: entityId,
                    title: entityName
                };
                institution.addEventListener("click", function (e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    var self = this;
                    SeamlessAccessService.updateEntity(entitydata).then(function (res) {
                        console.log(res);
                        window.location.href = self.href;
                    }).catch(function (err){
                        window.location.href = self.href;
                    });
                });
            });
        });

    </script>

                element = document.getElementsByClassName('').item(0);

          (event.slot.getSlotElementId() === "dfp-journal-asap-sponsor-2") || 
          (event.slot.getSlotElementId() === "dfp-pubs-search-sponsor-1") || 
          (event.slot.getSlotElementId() === "dfp-pubs-search-sponsor-2")) {
          if (event.isEmpty === false) {
            if(event.size) {
              $("#" + event.slot.getSlotElementId()).parents(".advertisement-container-toc").slideDown();
              $("#" + event.slot.getSlotElementId()).parents(".advertisement").slideDown();
              console.log("ad display: " + event.creativeId + " " + event.size[0] + "x" + event.size[1]);
            }
            else {
              $("#" + event.slot.getSlotElementId()).parents(".advertisement-container-toc").hide();
              $("#" + event.slot.getSlotElementId()).parents(".advertisement").hide();
            }
          }
        }
      }
    });
    googletag.enableServices();
  });
});
</script>





        
        <header class="header">



        
        <script type="text/javascript">
$(document).ready(function() {

  var revealerAdID = "#dfp-journal-hp-revealer";

  setTimeout(function() {
    googletag.cmd.push(function() {
      googletag.pubads().addEventListener("slotRenderEnded", function(event) {
        if (event.slot.getSlotElementId() === "dfp-journal-hp-revealer") {
          if(event.size) {
            if((event.size[0] === 1) && (event.size[1] === 1)) {
              $("header.header").css("position", "relative");
              $("main.content").css("margin-top", "0");
              $(revealerAdID).parents(".advertisement").slideDown();
              $(".pub-modal").css("z-index", "4");
              setTimeout(function() {
                revealerHeight = $(revealerAdID).parents(".advertisement").height();
                stickyHeader(revealerHeight);
              }, 1000);
            }
            else {  //event.size != 1x1
              $(revealerAdID).parents(".advertisement").remove();
              googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display("dfp-journal-hp-leaderboard"); });
              ("#dfp-journal-hp-leaderboard").parents(".advertisement.leaderboard").slideDown();
            }
          }
          else {  //event.size === null
            $(revealerAdID).parents(".advertisement").remove();
            googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display("dfp-journal-hp-leaderboard"); });
            $("#dfp-journal-hp-leaderboard").parents(".advertisement.leaderboard").slideDown();
          }
        }
      });
    });
  }, 1000);

  function stickyHeader(revealerHeight){
    var contentTopMargin = parseInt($("main.content").css("margin-top"));
    // var revealerOffset = revealerHeight + contentTopMargin + 1;
    var revealerOffset = parseInt($("header.header").height());
    var headerHeight = parseInt($("header.header").height()) - revealerHeight;

    $(window).scroll(function(){
      if($(revealerAdID).parents(".advertisement").height() <= 0) {
        $("header.header").css({
          "position": "fixed",
          "top": 0
        });
        $("main.content").css("margin-top", contentTopMargin + "px");
        $("main.content").offset({ top: headerHeight });
        $("footer.footer").css("margin-top", headerHeight + "px");
      }
      else {
        if($(this).scrollTop() >= revealerHeight){
          $("header.header").css({
            "position": "fixed", 
            "margin-top": "-" + revealerHeight + "px"
          });
          $("main.content").css("margin-top", contentTopMargin + "px");
          $("footer.footer").css("margin-top", revealerOffset + "px");
        }
        if($(this).scrollTop() < revealerHeight){
          $("header.header").css({
            "position": "relative",
            "margin-top": "0"
          });
          $("main.content").css("margin-top", "0");
        }
        $("main.content").offset({ top: revealerOffset });
      }
    });
  }

});
</script>

<div class="advertisement revealer">
  <div id="dfp-journal-hp-revealer">
    <script type="text/javascript">
      $(document).ready(function() {
        setTimeout(function() {
          googletag.cmd.push(function() { googletag.display("dfp-journal-hp-revealer"); });
        }, 1000);
      });
    </script>
  </div>
</div>

</style><script>$(function () {
    var jsonFile = "/pb-assets/json/journal-info-1617296739687.json";
    var coden = "aidcbc";
    var metricsFile = "/pb-assets/json/jcr-1593617698370.json";
    var relatedJournals = "/pb-assets/json/relatedJournals-1603744609413.json";
    var cobrandedJournals = "/pb-assets/json/cobranded-1551807476857.json";
    var oaJournals = "/pb-assets/json/oaJournals-1616525868993.json";
    var imagePath = "/pb-assets/images/" + coden + "/title-alt.png"; //For Alt images
    var latestIssue = "7";

    //Either show related journals of cobranding - script does not handle both
    if (coden == "jnprdf" || coden == "jceda8") {
      handleCobranding();
    } else {
      handleRelatedJournals();
    }

    // Check for Cobranded Journals
    function handleCobranding() {
      $.getJSON(cobrandedJournals)
          .done(function (cbData) {
            console.log(cbData);
            var relatedList = $('.jhHeader_relatedList ul');
            $('.readRelated span:first-child').text('ACS Division'); //Update btn text
            var coBrandData = cbData.copublished;
            for (var j = 0; j < coBrandData.length; j++) {
              if ( coBrandData[j].coden == coden ) {
                  cpackage(coBrandData[j].journ_name);
                  $('.jh_line').show();
                  break;
              } 
            }     
            function cpackage(name) {
           
                var listItem = $('<li/>', { class:"jhHeader_relatedItem cobrand"});
                if (coden === 'jceda8') {
                   listItem.append('<a href="'+name.jlink+'" title="'+name.jtitle+'"><img class="cobrand_wide" src='+name.jlogo+'/><span>'+ name.jtitle+'</span></a>');
                } else {
                   listItem.append('<a href="'+name.jlink+'" title="'+name.jtitle+'"><img src='+name.jlogo+'/><span>'+ name.jtitle+'</span></a>');
                } 
               
                relatedList.append(listItem);
            }
      });  
    }
    //Will not run if the journal has cobranding
     
    // Check for related journals
    function handleRelatedJournals() {
      $.getJSON(relatedJournals)
        .done(function (rjData) {
          var relatedList = $('.jhHeader_relatedList ul');
          var relatedData = rjData.relatedJournals;
          for (var j = 0; j < relatedData.length; j++) {
            if ( relatedData[j].coden.indexOf(coden) !== -1) {
              package(relatedData[j].journ_name);
              $('.jh_line').show();
              break;
            } else {
              $('.jhHeader_logo').css('width', '100%');
            }
          }     
          function package(names) {
            names.sort();
            for ( var i = 0; i < names.length; i++) {
              var listItem = $('<li/>', { class:"jhHeader_relatedItem"});
              var Jname = names[i].split('|');
              var Jcode = Jname[1].replace(/\s/g, '');
              if (Jcode === coden) {
                continue;
              } else {
                listItem.append('<a href="/journal/'+Jcode +'">' + Jname[0] + '</a>');
                relatedList.append(listItem);
              }
            }
          }
        })
        .fail(function() {
          console.log("relatedJournals.json error");
        });   
    }

    // Check for Alt Image
    $.get(imagePath)
      .done(function(data) { 
        //console.log("file exist");
        if (data) {
           $('.jhHeader_logo img').attr('src', imagePath);
           $('.jhHeader_logo img').show();
        } else {
          $('.jhHeader_logo img').show();
        }
      }).fail(function(data) { 
        $('.jhHeader_logo img').show();
        // Do nothing - file does not exist
        //Tasks - hide intial image then show here
      });

    // Get Editor Data
    $.getJSON(jsonFile)
        .done(function (jdata) {
            var editors = jdata.journalInfo.journal[coden].editor;
            var editorNames = $('span.hdr_editors');
            var titleCount = 0;
            var editorCount = 0;
            var editorList;

            for(titles in editors) {
                editorList = '<span class="editor_group"><span class="editor_title">' + titles + ':&nbsp;</span>';
                for(names in editors[titles]) {
                    if((editorCount == 0) && (names == 0)) {
                        editorList += '<span><a href="/page/' + coden + '/profile.html" title="About the Editor">';
                    } else if((editorCount > 0) && (names == 0)) {
                        editorList += '<span><a href="/page/' + coden + '/profile' + editorCount + '.html" title="About the Editor">';
                    } else {
                        editorList += ', <span><a href="/page/' + coden + '/profile' + editorCount + '.html" title="About the Editor">';
                    }
                    editorList += '<strong>' + editors[titles][names] + '</strong></a></span>';
                    editorCount++;
                }
                editorList += '</span>';
                editorNames.append(editorList);
                titleCount++;
            }
        });

    // Get Impact data
    if(latestIssue > 3) {
      $.getJSON(metricsFile)
          .done(function (mdata) {
              //console.log(mdata);
              var year = mdata.jcr.year;
              var citationData = mdata.jcr.journal[coden].citations;
              var impactData = mdata.jcr.journal[coden].impact;
              //console.log(citationData , impactData)
              var impactArea = $('span.jhHeader_impact');
              var citationArea =  $('span.jhHeader_citations');
              if (citationData.length > 1 && impactData.length > 1) {                
                   impactArea.text("Impact Factor " +  year + ": " + impactData);
                   $('.jh_spacer').text(" | ");
                   citationArea.text("Citations " + year + ": " + citationData);
              } 
          });
    }
    
    // Check for Open Access
    $.get(oaJournals)
      .done(function(OAdata) { 
        //console.log("oaJournals file exist");
        var oaList = OAdata.oaJournals;
        if (oaList.indexOf(coden) > -1) {
          //console.log("this is an OA journal");
          var oaLogo = "/pb-assets/images/openaccess/OA_Icon-1616525985103.png";
          var oaLogo2 = "/pb-assets/images/openaccess/OA_Icon_alt-1616525984767.png"
          var oaLink = "https://acsopenscience.org/";
          var oaIconContainer = $("<div/>", { "id": "oaLogo" });
          var oaIconLink = $("<a></a>", { 
            "href": oaLink,
            "title": "ACS Open Science"
          });
          var oaIconImage = $("<img></img>", { 
            "src": oaLogo, 
            "class": "primary",
            "alt": "ACS Open Science logo"
          });
          var oaIconImage2 = $("<img></img>", { 
            "src": oaLogo2, 
            "class": " secondary",
            "alt": "ACS Open Science logo"
          });
          $(oaIconLink).clone().addClass("primary").append(oaIconImage).appendTo(oaIconContainer);
          $(oaIconLink).clone().addClass("secondary").append(oaIconImage2).appendTo(oaIconContainer);
          $(".jhHeader_lowerleft").prepend(oaIconContainer);
          $(".jhHeader_lowerleft").addClass("oaJournal");

          var oaSmallImage = $("<img></img>", {
            "src": oaLogo2,
            "class": "small",
            "alt": "ACS Open Science logo"
          });
          var oaButton = $(".button_primary_2.jhHeader_sub_info");
          oaButton.each(function() {
            //if($(this).hasAttr("title") === "Subscription information") {
            if(!$(this).hasClass("niHeader_getEAlerts")) {
              $(this).addClass("open_science");
              $(this).attr("href", oaLink);
              $(this).children(".icon-file-text").remove();
              $(oaSmallImage).prependTo($(this));
              $(this).children("span").text("Open Science");
            }
          });
        }
      }).fail(function(OAdata) { 
        // Do nothing - file does not exist
        //Tasks - hide intial image then show here
      });
  
    //Event Handlers 
    $('.readRelated').on('click', function(event) {
        event.preventDefault();
        event.stopPropagation();
        $('.jhHeader_relatedList').toggleClass('show');
    });
    $(window).click(function() {
      $('.jhHeader_relatedList').removeClass('show');
    });

    //Display Current Issue after vol. 1 is available
    if ((latestIssue >= 1)) {
      $('#main-nav-list #nav-loi').show();
      $('#main-nav-list #nav-current').show();
      $('.current_issue').slideDown();

      //Add reprint button to Current Issue section
      if ( $('#reprint-jhp').length ) {
        vol = "7";
        iss = "4";
        $('#reprint-jhp').attr('href', 'http://pubstore.acs.org/file.aspx?&n=' + coden + '&v=' + vol + '&i=' + iss);
        $('#reprint-jhp').css("display","inline-block");
      }
    }

    //Check if element on page is ready (ASAPs/Most Read/Editors' Choice)
    function elementReady(selector) {
      return new Promise(function (resolve, reject) {
        var el = document.querySelector(selector);

        if (el) {
          resolve(el);
        }

        new MutationObserver(function (mutationRecords, observer) {
          // Query for elements matching the specified selector
          [].slice.call(document.querySelectorAll(selector)).forEach(function (element) {
            resolve(element); //Once we have resolved we don't need the observer anymore.

            observer.disconnect();
          });
        }).observe(document.documentElement, {
          childList: true,
          subtree: true
        });
      });
    } //Display ASAPs section if there are articles 


    elementReady('.journal-home_section.asap_articles .owl-item').then(function () {
      if ($('.journal-home_section.asap_articles .owl-item').length > 1) {
        $('.col-xs-12.asap-articles').slideDown();
        $('#main-nav-list #nav-asap').show();
      }
    }); //Display Most Read section if there are articles

    elementReady('.journal-home_section.most_read_articles .owl-item').then(function () {
      if ($('.journal-home_section.most_read_articles .owl-item').length > 1) {
        $('.col-xs-12.most-read').slideDown();
      }
    }); //Display Editors' Choice section if there are articles

    elementReady('.journal-home_section.editors_choice_articles .owl-item').then(function () {
      if ($('.journal-home_section.editors_choice_articles .owl-item').length > 1) {
        $('.col-xs-12.editors-choice').slideDown();
      }
    });
});  

</script><div class="jhHeader"><div class="container container_scaled-down"><div class="row"><div class="col-xs-12"><div class="jhHeader_content"><div class="jhHeader_left col-lg-6 clearfix"><div class="jhHeader_upperLeft"><div class="jhHeader_logo"><h1><a href="/journal/aidcbc" aria-label="ACS Infectious Diseases homepage"><img src="/na101/home/literatum/publisher/achs/journals/covergifs/aidcbc/title.png" alt="ACS Infectious Diseases"></a></h1></div><div class="jh_line"><!-- a.readRelated(href='/action/recommendation?doi=10.1021/'+ data.journal.code, title='Recommend this Journal')--><a href="#" title="Related Journals" class="readRelated"><span>Related Journals</span><span> <i class="fa icon-angle-down"></i></span></a><div class="jhHeader_relatedList"><ul></ul></div></div></div><div class="jhHeader_lowerleft"><div class="jhHeader-editor__area"><p><span class="hdr_editors"> </span><span class="hdr_editorial"> <!-- span.editor_spacer | --><span><a href="/page/aidcbc/editors.html">Editors & Editorial Board</a></span></span></p></div><input type="hidden" name="journalCodeForMetrics"><div class="jhHeader_metrics"><span class="jhHeader_impact"></span><span class="jh_spacer"></span><span class="jhHeader_citations"></span></div></div></div><div class="jhHeader_right col-md-6 clearfix"><div class="jhHeader_coverWrap"><a href="/toc/aidcbc/7/4"><img src="/action/showCoverImage?journalCode=aidcbc" alt="Cover"></a><div class="jhHeader_meta"><span>Volume 7</span><span>Issue 4</span><p class="jhHeader__date">April 9, 2021</p></div></div><div class="jhHeader_buttons"><a href="https://acs.manuscriptcentral.com/acs" title="Submit Manuscript" class="button_primary_2 jhHeader_submitManuscript"><i class="icon-file-text"></i><span>Submit Manuscript</span></a><a href="/page/4librarians/subscriptions/index.html" title="Subscription information" class="button_primary_2 jhHeader_sub_info"><i class="icon-file-text"></i><span>Subscriber Info</span></a>

    //console.log(elem)
    // Make sure an element and number of items to truncate is provided
    if (!elem || !limit) return;

    // Get the inner content of the element
    var content = elem.trim();

    //Convert to array 
    content = content.split(' ');

    //If number of words > limit
    if (content.length >= limit) {
        content = content.slice(0, limit);
        // Convert to string and add after elem 
        content = content.join(' ') + (after ? after : '');
    } else {
        content = content.join(' ');
    }
    return content;
};

 var changeDate = function(d) {
       const monthNames = ["January", "February", "March", "April", "May", "June",
              "July", "August", "September", "October", "November", "December"
            ];

       var monthShortNames = ["Jan", "Feb", "Mar", "Apr", "May", "Jun",
        "Jul", "Aug", "Sep", "Oct", "Nov", "Dec"
      ];

      d = d.split(' ');
      var Month = monthNames[monthShortNames.indexOf(d[2])]; //gets index of short name, displays long name
        var date = Month+ " " + d[1].toString() +", "+ d[3].toString();
        return date; 
  };

//takes the rss feed on the dom as input
//output is the class of each box to write to.
var buildList_CEN = function(input, output) {

    if ($(input + ' .listOfPublications li').length > 0) {
        $(input).show();
    } else {
        return false;
    }
    $(input).find('.listOfPublications li').each(function(index, article) {
         console.log(article);
        // var title = $(article).find('a').attr('title');
        var title = title = truncate($(article).find('a').text(), 5, '...');
        var image = $(article).find('img').attr('src');
        var link = $(article).find('a').attr('href');
        var date = changeDate( $(article).find('div.published').text() );
        var author = $(article).find('div.author').text();
        // console.log(image);
        // console.log(link);
        // console.log(title);

        var elem = $('<a/>', {
            href: link
        });
        if (image !== undefined) {
            elem.append($('<div class="cen-img-wrap"></div>').css('background-image', 'url(' + image + ')'));
            elem.append('<p>' + title + '</p>');
            elem.append('<p class="cen-date">'+ date+'</p>');
            //elem.append('<p class="cen-author">'+ author+'</p>');
        } else {
            $(output + (index + 1)).addClass('no-image');
            elem.append('<p>' + title + '</p>');
            elem.append('<p class="cen-date">'+ date+'</p>');
            //elem.append('<p class="cen-author">'+ author+'</p>');

            $(output + (index + 1)).append('<div class="cen_box-bottom"><img src="/pb-assets/images/CEN-Logo-1490205552357.png"></img></div>');
        }
        
        

        $(output + (index + 1)).append(elem);
    });
}

$(document).ready(function() {
    setTimeout(function() {
        buildList_CEN('.cenge_wrap', '.cen-item-');
    }, 1600);
});
</script>

</div>
</div>
</div>

        </div>

<script>


    //Axial Script
    var truncate = function (elem, limit, after) {
        //console.log(elem)
        // Make sure an element and number of items to truncate is provided
        if (!elem || !limit) return;

        // Get the inner content of the element
        var content = elem.trim();

        //Convert to array 
        content = content.split(' ');

        //If number of words > limit
        if (content.length >= limit) {
           content =  content.slice(0, limit);
            // Convert to string and add after elem 
           content = content.join(' ') + (after ? after : '');
        } else {
          content = content.join(' ');
        } 
      

        return content;
      
    };

    var changeDate = function(d) {
       const monthNames = ["January", "February", "March", "April", "May", "June",
              "July", "August", "September", "October", "November", "December"
            ];

       var monthShortNames = ["Jan", "Feb", "Mar", "Apr", "May", "Jun",
        "Jul", "Aug", "Sep", "Oct", "Nov", "Dec"
      ];

      d = d.split(' ');
      var Month = monthNames[monthShortNames.indexOf(d[2])]; //gets index of short name, displays long name
        var date = Month+ " " + d[1].toString() +", "+ d[3].toString();
        return date; 
    }

      //takes the rss feed on the dom as input
      //output is the class of each box to write to.
      
      function buildList(input, output) {
            
            if ($(input + ' .listOfPublications li').length > 0) {
              $(input).show();
            } else {
              return false;
            }

            $(input).find('.listOfPublications li').each(function(index, article) { 
              //console.log(index);
              //console.log(article);
             // var title = $(article).find('a').attr('title');
              var title = title = truncate($(article).find('a').text(), 5, '...');
             var image = $(article).find('img').attr('src');

              var link = $(article).find('a').attr('href');
              var date = changeDate( $(article).find('div.published').text() );
              //console.log(date);
                /* console.log(image);
                 console.log(link);
                 console.log(title);*/

             var elem = $('<a/>', { href: link });
            if (image !== undefined  ) {
              elem.append($('<div class="ax-img-wrap"></div>').css('background-image', 'url(' + image + ')')); 
              
            } else {
              $( output+ (index+1)).addClass('no-image');
              $(output+ (index+1)).append('<div class="axial_box-bottom"><img src="/pb-assets/images/axial/axial-white-1551216432197.png"></img></div>');
            }
            
            
             elem.append('<p>'+ title +'</p>');
             elem.append('<p class="ax-date">'+ date+'</p>');
             
             $(output+ (index+1)).append(elem);
                 
            });
     
  }

        setTimeout(function() {
            var cookieExist = getCookie("gdpr");
            if (cookieExist) {
                //console.log("gdpr cookie exist");
                return false;
            } else {
                //console.log("gdpr cookie does not exist")
                gdprMessage();
            }
            //Events
            $('#closebtn').on("click", hideForm);

            //Handle submit
            $('#gdpr-message-btn').on("click", function(event) {
                handleClick();
            });

            // //Hide if clicked outside div - TO DO stop handling click after submit
            // $(document).click(function(event) {
            // 	event.stopPropagation();
            //   console.log(event.target);
            //   if (!$(event.target).closest("#gdpr-message-content").length) {
            //     $("body").find("#gdpr-message-modal").hide();
            //     $(this).off();
            //   }
            // });
            $('#gdpr-con-btn').click(function() {
                setCookie("gdpr", "true");
                hideForm();
            });
        }, time);
    }

    //Show the message
    function gdprMessage() {
        //console.log("Show GDPR Message");
        var tMessage, emailInput, messageButton, ewrap;

        $('#gdpr-message-modal').show();
    }

    function handleClick() {
        //console.log($("#gdpr-input").val());
        emailValid = validateEmail($("#gdpr-input").val());
        if (emailValid) {
            //Submit the form
            //Hide form
            if ($('.gdpr_err')) {
                $('.gdpr_err').hide();
            }

            $("#gdpr-message-content")
                //If successful then...
            setCookie("gdpr", "true");
            //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid + " submiting form");
        } else {
            //Show error message
            gdprErrorMessage();
            //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid);
        }
    }

    function gdprErrorMessage() {
        if (errorStatus) {
            return false;
        } else {
            errorStatus = true;
            $("#gdpr-message-content").append(errormessage);
        }
    }

    function validateEmail(email) {
        var re = /^(([^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+(\.[^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+)*)|(".+"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
        return re.test(String(email).toLowerCase());
    }

    function setCookie(name, value) {
        var expires = "";
        expires = "; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT";
        document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "") + expires + "; path=/";
    }

    function getCookie(name) {
        var match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp(name + '=([^;]+)'));
        if (match) return match[1];
    }

    function hideForm() { //And set cookie
        $('#gdpr-message-modal').hide();
        setCookie("gdpr", "false");
        ga('send', 'event', 'Pubs GDPR', 'GDPR Modal', 'GDPR Dismissal');
    }

    return {
        init: init
    }
})();

$(document).ready(infoCentralCapture.init);
</script>

        <!-- COVID-19 Remote Access message -->
<script>
$(document).ready(function(){
    var messageContainer = $("<div/>", {id: "sitewide-message"});
    var innerContainer = $("<div/>", {class: "row container container_scaled-down"});
    $(innerContainer).html("<strong>COVID-19 Remote Access Support:</strong> <a href='/page/remoteaccess'>Learn More</a> about expanded access to ACS Publications research.");
    $(messageContainer).append(innerContainer);

    if (window.location.href.indexOf("/page/remoteaccess") > -1) {
        return;
    }
    // C&EN pages
    else if ($("header").hasClass("header-CandEN")) {
        var currentDOI = "";
        if ($("main").hasClass("cen-hp")) {
            $(messageContainer).prependTo(".cen-hp-topSection").slideDown();
        }
        else if($("main").hasClass("article")) {
            // C&EN Archive articles
            if(currentDOI.indexOf("10.1021/cen-v") > -1) {
                $(messageContainer).prependTo("article").slideDown();
            }
            // C&EN Global Enterprise articles
            else {
                $(messageContainer).prependTo(".cen-article-page").slideDown();
            }
        }
        // C&EN Global Enterprise TOC, LOI, about
        else if ((window.location.href.indexOf("/loi/cgeabj/") > -1) || (window.location.href.indexOf("/toc/cgeabj/") > -1) || (window.location.href.indexOf("/cgeabj/about") > -1)) {
            $(messageContainer).css("margin-top","142px");
            $(messageContainer).prependTo("main.content").slideDown();
        }
        // C&EN Archive TOC
        else if (window.location.href.indexOf("/toc/cenear/") > -1) {
            $(messageContainer).css("margin-top","32px");
            $(messageContainer).prependTo("main.content").slideDown();
        }
    }
    else if ($("main").hasClass("styleguide-chapter")) {
        // $(".article_header").css("padding-top", "0");
        $(messageContainer).prependTo(".article_content").slideDown();
    }
    else if ($("main").hasClass("article")) {
        $(".article_header").css("padding-top", "0");
        $(messageContainer).insertAfter(".articleHeaderDropzone5").slideDown();
    }
    else if ($("main").hasClass("journal-home")) {
        $(messageContainer).prependTo(".home_header").slideDown();
    }
    else if ($("#dfp-vi-leaderboard").length) {
        if ($(".cpJournalHeader").length) {
            $(messageContainer).insertBefore(".cpJournalHeader").slideDown();
        }
        else {
            $(messageContainer).insertBefore($(".vi-content-wrapper").parents(".container")).slideDown();
        }
    }
    else {
        $(messageContainer).prependTo("main.content").slideDown();
    }
});
</script>
